 is kit main machharadaani, metress, ek jodi kapade, napkin, tel kii shishi, baby shampoo , sabundani ke saath ek sabun, nail-kattar, ratel toy or hand senetizer jaise kul 16 jaruri saamaan hai

 Amol was very disappointed at that time
 unhone kaha tha ki auskar main lobing behad jaruri he
 Very few people will know that at the age of 17, Miss India became Bollywood's heroine Meenakshi Seshadri
 vah apane samay kii top actress main shumaar raheen
 Meenakshi gave hit films like 'ghayal', 'deadly' and 'damini' but Meenakshi suddenly distanced herself from films
 vah kai saalon baad ek aword function main ain or media ke saamne unhone apane jivan se jude kai khulaase kiye
 Let's know
 aap kai saalon baad hamase rubaru ho rahi hai, kahaan thi aap or kisi hai or aapaki hindi kisi he?main acchhee hum, aajkal uese main rahati hum
 Actually i am from Delhi
 meri hindi thik hi he or hindi akhbaar padhakar or bhi acchhee hindi bolne kii koshish karti hum
 Why are you away from films? Are there any plans to return to films? i have not worked in films for so many years because i have given more priority to both my children and family
 abhi bhi mere bachche skool main hai or main sochati hum ki jab meri beti graduate ho jaayegi to shaayad main us vakt kuch karne kaa sochoongi

 All the things or news that were going on till now are just news, yes such things were going on that i will be seen in 'wounded 2' but it has not happened yet

 agar wo parmishan denge to jarur sochoongi

 Public sector Indian Oil Corporation (IOC) has become the highest profit making public sector company for the second consecutive year
 usne tel evam gas kaa utpaadan karne vaali oengisi ko bhi chhod diya he
 After IOC has been in the highest profit, questions have arisen as to why the company should be given subsidy to sell fuel cheaply amid rising prices of petrol and diesel
 haal main is tarah kii reportein ai thi ki sarkaar oengisi tathaa tel, gas utpaadan se judi duusari companiyon ko sabsidi main yogadan ke liye kah sakati he
 IOC was the largest company in the country in terms of business for decades
 iosi kaa shuddh laabh vitt varsh 2017-18 main 12 pratishat badhkar 21,346 karod rupee rahaa
 Earlier, it stood at Rs 19,106 crore in the financial year
 company ne pichley saptaah hi vittiya parinaam kii ghoshnaa kii
 Oil and Natural Gas Corporation (ONGC) net profit of 11 in 2017-18
 4 pratishat badhkar 19,945 karod rupee rahaa
 However, Reliance Industries, led by veteran businessman Mukesh Ambani, remained the most valuable company for the third consecutive year
 company kaa munafa 36,075 karod rupee rahaa
 The country's largest software company Tata Consultancy Services had a net profit of Rs 25,580 crore in 2017-18 and became the second most valuable company
 oengisi lambey samay tak sarvaadhik laabh kamaane vaali company rahi lekin teen saal pehle nijee kshetra kii reliance or tisies se yah pichad gayi
 In fact, ONGC leverages three public sector retail companies
 
 
 indian aayal corporation (iosi) , hindustan petroleum karporation li 
 (HPCL) and Bharat Petroleum Corporation Ltd
 (bipisiel) ke sanyukt laabh se bhi adhik tha 
 But now she lags behind the IOC

 43 lakh crores
 vahiin bipisiel kaa shuddh laabh pichley vitt varsh main 7,919 karod rupee rahaa
 The retailing companies of petroleum products like IOC, HPCL and BPCL are making good profits, in which case ONGC and Oil India have been asked to ask them to contribute subsidy on selling petrol, diesel at cheap price
 
 tippaniyan a senior ONGC official said, "look at their profit
 unhen kisi sabsidi samarthan kii jarurat nahin he

 ) You might not believe that comedian Kapil Sharma, who makes people around the world laugh and entertains everyone, is also an elder brother who stays absolutely serious and guards the AK-47 Tane Pathankot airbase
 ji haa, yakeen karnaa mushkil he, lekin sachai yahi he kikamedian kapil sharmaake bade bhai ashok sharma apni jeevika chalaane ke liye koi hansi-majaak nahin karte hai
 Ever since the jaish-e-mohammed militants attacked Pathankot airbase on 2 January, Ashok Sharma has been standing in the security of this sensitive defense facility
 kandhe par eke-47 taane ashok ko dekhakar koi nahin kah saktaa ki wo world femescomedian kapil sharmaake bade bhai hai
 Ashok takes his work very seriously
 ashok multah amritsar police main ek head consteble ke taur par kaam karte hai lekin 2 janvari ko pathankot airbase par hamale ke baad lagbhag 80 pulisavaalon ke saath unhen bhi airbase bheja gaya
 Ashok, along with his comrades, surrounded the airbase from all sides, so that the terrorists could not escape
 ashok bataate hai, 'pehle teen din hamane rojaanaa 20-ghante kii shift kii he
 We would take a break just for a nap and a tea-biscuit and again the same routine
 hamale ke samay ham log samaj nahin paa rahe the ki kis par hamalaa karen, kyunki aatankiyon ne bhi hamaari tarah army kii dress pahani hui thi
 'although Ashok is about 2 years older than his younger brother Kapil, but both look very similar
 unke pita jatinder kumaar bhi ek pulicekarmi the or punjab police main sab-inspector the
 He died of cancer in 2004
 ashok bataate hai kikapil ke sho par wo rishi kapur, amitabh bachchan or salmaan khan jaise kai celebrities se mil chuke hai
 Private sector Axis Bank has acquired Inam Securities' investment banking arm in a deal worth Rs 2,067 crore
 saude ke tahat inaam securities kii nivesh banking ikai, karporate salaahkaar sevaayen or equity vitaran ikai exis bank ke paas chali gai hai
 The deal excludes Inam Securities' asset management company and insurance broking unit
 exis bank kii prabandh nideshak shikha sharma ne yahaan samvaadadaataaon se kaha, ‚Äò‚Äòhamen bharosa he ki ranneetik drushti se yah kaaphi acha sauda he
 He said that for this, shares worth Rs 2,067 crore of Axis Bank will be given to Inam Securities
 sharma ne kaha ki bhartiya rigerv bank tathaa bhartiya pratibhuti evam vinimay board :sebi: kii niamak manjuuri hasil hone ke baad hi yah sauda puraa hoga
 Axis Bank is the premier private sector bank in the country
 deshbhar main bank kii 1,000 shakhaon kaa network he
 Inam Securities was formed in 1984 as a financial services provider company
 duniya kii sabase choti car ke bare main jaanate hai aap? ho saktaa he jaanate bhi hon lekin ye to bilkul nahin jaanate honge ki yah car sadak par nahin rail kii patariyon par chalati he
 This car made in Britain is made by Forfour
